loss = loss_target_total*0.2 + loss_exa_total

loss_target_input = loss_ce * (1 - 0.5) + loss_ce_soft * 0.5 + loss_tri_soft + (loss_dist + loss_lf_tri)*adaptive_lamda
其中：adaptive_lamda examplar为1， target_dataset=0.5
目标是为了测试（在新数据上面比较高的蒸馏损失	Loss_lf 4.076 / 2.955是否有效果。）
发现将蒸馏损失系数变小，没有用处

  self.calculate_loss(target_inputs,self.old_class_num,self.total_class_num,0.5,self.criterion_ce1,cal_dist= use_dist,T=2)#lamda

                loss_exa_total, loss_ce_exa, loss_ce_soft_exa, loss_tri_soft_exa, loss_dist_exa,loss_dist_tri_exa,pre_exa = \
                self.calculate_loss(examplar_inputs, 0, self.total_class_num, 1,self.criterion_ce2, cal_dist=use_dist,T=2)#lamda
